<hr>
<h2>7. Security notes</h2>
<h3><code>web_fetch</code></h3>
<ul>
<li>Blocks <code>file:</code> protocol (<code>keyword-engine__0617.js:2302</code>)</li>
<li>URL permission prompt when <code>requestRequired</code></li>
<li>10 MB byte stream cap (<code>Fys</code>), 20k char return cap (<code>usr</code>)</li>
<li>No custom auth headers in <code>Ler</code> fetch (<code>headers: {}</code>)</li>
</ul>
<h3>MCP <code>web_search</code></h3>
<ul>
<li>Requires <code>GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN</code> bearer (<code>client-registry.js:28</code>)</li>
<li>Tool exposure gated by <code>X-MCP-Toolsets</code> and optional <code>X-MCP-Exclude-Tools</code></li>
</ul>
<h3>Telemetry</h3>
<p>Renamed MCP tool sets <code>safeForTelemetry: true</code> on the <code>web_search</code> alias (<code>C9t</code>).</p>
<p><code>web_fetch</code> also sets <code>safeForTelemetry: true</code> on tool definition (<code>keyword-engine__0617.js:2265</code>). Telemetry uses hashed URL in properties while retaining restricted full URL for debugging (<code>:2279-2282</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>7b. Operational workflow (agent perspective)</h2>
<p>Typical multi-step web research in Copilot CLI:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Discovery</strong> — call <code>web_search</code> (hosted or MCP) with natural-language query; UI shows <code>Searching for '…'</code> (<code>keyword-engine__1526.js:396-399</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Deep read</strong> — call <code>web_fetch</code> on a result URL; markdown default simplifies HTML for token efficiency.</li>
<li><strong>Pagination</strong> — if response includes <code>&#x3C;note>Content truncated. Call the fetch tool with a start_index of N&#x3C;/note></code>, continue with <code>start_index=N</code> (<code>keyword-engine__0617.js:2339-2343</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Permission</strong> — first fetch to a domain may block on <code>permissions.request</code> until user approves (<code>:2309-2321</code>).</li>
</ol>
<p>This differs from OpenCode where <code>websearch</code> returns MCP blob text in one shot and <code>webfetch</code> is a separate Effect tool — Copilot's <code>web_fetch</code> pagination is more explicit in the tool contract.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 015_reverse-engineering/ (심화)</h2>
<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/00_reverse_evidence_policy.md</code></h3>
<h1>Reverse Engineering Evidence Policy</h1>
<p>이 축은 설치 help parity 문서의 다음 단계다. 기존 <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> 축은 주로 help/config/local-doc 표면을 비교했고, 이 축은 설치된 바이너리와 번들에서 복원 가능한 구조를 따로 기록한다.</p>
<h2>Evidence Levels</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Level</th>
<th>의미</th>
<th>사용할 수 있는 주장</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>installed-help</td>
<td><code>--help</code>, public command output, version output</td>
<td>명령/플래그/공개 subcommand가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>safe-local-doc</td>
<td>설치 패키지의 docs, changelog, examples, manifest</td>
<td>문서화된 schema/경로/기능 설명이 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bundle-key</td>
<td>minified bundle에 남은 module key, source path, route name, proto name</td>
<td>내부 모듈/라우터/프로토/컴포넌트가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>binary-string</td>
<td>native binary <code>strings</code>, <code>file</code>, <code>otool</code>, <code>codesign</code>, <code>nm</code></td>
<td>crate/package/protocol/tool/evaluator 이름이 embedded되어 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>runtime-trace</td>
<td>synthetic project에서 실제 명령을 실행한 결과</td>
<td>동작 semantics, precedence, permission enforcement를 확인했다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>private-artifact-name</td>
<td>비공개 상태 파일의 경로/개수만 관찰</td>
<td>artifact가 존재한다. 내용/schema 주장은 금지</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/015_reverse-engineering/33_source_deobfuscation_inventory.md</code> further separates source-like recovery levels. In this corpus, Cursor reaches preserved module-key recovery, while Grok/Kiro/AGY mostly expose native source-path, handler, protobuf, and runtime-trace evidence. Do not call this "full source recovered" unless a real source map or readable source archive is present.</p>
<h2>Hard Boundary</h2>
<p>역분석의 목적은 제품 구조 복원이지 사용자 상태 추출이 아니다. 다음은 내용 읽기 금지다.</p>
<ul>
<li>auth/token/cookie/credential/login data</li>
<li>raw transcript, chat history, conversation DB/PB</li>
<li>logs and terminal captures</li>
<li>browser profile state, local storage, IndexedDB, session storage</li>
<li>memory/goal runtime stores</li>
<li>screenshots and browser recordings</li>
<li>private <code>mcp.json</code>, settings, config values unless explicitly redacted</li>
</ul>
<p>비공개 artifact는 “존재한다”까지만 쓴다. 필드/schema/content 주장은 public docs, source/bundle evidence, sanitized fixture, synthetic runtime trace가 있을 때만 쓴다.</p>
<h2>Installed CLI version pin (2026-06-27)</h2>
<p>Single source of truth for pinned <code>ay</code>/<code>cr</code>/<code>gr</code>/<code>ki</code> binaries:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/015_reverse-engineering/36_installed_cli_version_manifest.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p>WP5 trace shards (<code>38</code>–<code>41</code>) extend hubs without changing evidence-level definitions above.</p>

<h2>Reading Rule For Existing Docs</h2>
<p>When a <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> page says “없음” or “지원하지 않음”, interpret it as “installed help에서 노출되지 않음” unless this <code>15_reverse-engineering</code> axis confirms absence from bundle/binary evidence too.</p>
<p>When a page states runtime semantics from config/cache observation, this axis upgrades or downgrades the claim:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>bundle-key</code> or <code>binary-string</code> confirms a module exists.</li>
<li><code>runtime-trace</code> is still required for exact precedence, scheduling, isolation, merge, and permission behavior.</li>
</ul>

<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/24_ki_agent_mcp_trace.md</code></h3>
<h1>Kiro Agent MCP Trace</h1>
<p>This pass used disposable temp <code>HOME</code> and workspace directories. It did not run model prompts, start real MCP servers, authenticate, or read private Kiro sessions.</p>
<h2>Public Help Surface</h2>
<p>Commands inspected:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>/Users/jun/.local/bin/kiro-cli-chat agent create --help</code></li>

<li><code>/Users/jun/.local/bin/kiro-cli-chat mcp list --help</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Relevant help semantics:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>agent create [NAME] --directory &#x3C;DIRECTORY></code> creates an agent config in the chosen directory, but opens an editor by default.</li>
<li><code>agent list</code> says local agents are discovered only when invoked in a directory that contains them.</li>
<li><code>mcp add --agent &#x3C;AGENT></code> writes the server to the named agent.</li>
<li><code>mcp add --scope &#x3C;SCOPE></code> is only meaningful when no agent name is supplied.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Editor Behavior</h2>
<p><code>agent create trace --directory &#x3C;tmp>/ws/.kiro/agents</code> created <code>&#x3C;tmp>/ws/.kiro/agents/trace.json</code> and opened it in <code>vi</code>. The generated template shape was:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">{
  "name": "trace",
  "description": "",
  "prompt": null,
  "mcpServers": {},
  "tools": ["*"],
  "toolAliases": {},
  "allowedTools": [],
  "resources": [],
  "hooks": {},
  "toolsSettings": {},
  "includeMcpJson": true,
  "model": null
}
</code></pre>
<p>The editor process was terminated after capturing the template. Follow-up traces used a directly written synthetic JSON file with the same shape to avoid interactive editor state.</p>

<h2>Minimal Fixture</h2>
<p>Synthetic workspace:</p>
<ul>
<li>temp workspace: <code>/tmp/cursor-mcp-final.DLswue/ws</code></li>
<li>temp HOME: <code>/tmp/cursor-mcp-final.DLswue/home</code></li>

<p>The config shape was:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">{"mcpServers":{"trace":{"command":"/Users/jun/.nvm/versions/node/v24.14.1/bin/node","args":["/tmp/cursor-mcp-final.DLswue/trace-mcp.js"]}}}
</code></pre>
<p>The synthetic server was a no-network stdio process that logged startup, parsed <code>Content-Length</code> JSON-RPC frames, answered <code>initialize</code>, and returned one tool from <code>tools/list</code>.</p>
<h2>Approval Flow</h2>
<p>Command:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">HOME=/tmp/cursor-mcp-final.DLswue/home /Users/jun/.local/bin/cursor-agent mcp enable trace
</code></pre>
<p>from the temp workspace returned:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">✓ Enabled and approved MCP server: trace
</code></pre>
<p>Cursor Agent wrote:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">[
  "trace-0bab3cead8c72734"
]
</code></pre>
<p>Implications:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>mcp enable</code> uses the current working directory, not only <code>--workspace</code>, to resolve project MCP config.</li>
<li>Project approval state is stored under temp HOME at <code>.cursor/projects/&#x3C;project-slug>/mcp-approvals.json</code>.</li>
<li>The approval key is derived from the server name, server config, and project root. The trace observed <code>trace-0bab3cead8c72734</code> for this fixture.</li>
</ul>

<h2>Official MCP Server Success Trace</h2>
<p>To separate a fixture implementation issue from Cursor's MCP loader behavior, a second temp workspace used the official <code>@modelcontextprotocol/server-everything</code> package through <code>npx</code> with an isolated npm cache:</p>
<ul>
<li>temp workspace: <code>/tmp/cursor-mcp-official.onq9Rl/ws</code></li>
<li>temp HOME: <code>/tmp/cursor-mcp-official.onq9Rl/home</code></li>
<li>npm cache: <code>/tmp/cursor-mcp-official.onq9Rl/npm-cache</code></li>
<li>config file: <code>/tmp/cursor-mcp-official.onq9Rl/ws/.cursor/mcp.json</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Config shape:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">{"mcpServers":{"everything":{"command":"/Users/jun/.nvm/versions/node/v24.14.1/bin/npx","args":["-y","@modelcontextprotocol/server-everything"],"env":{"npm_config_cache":"/tmp/cursor-mcp-official.onq9Rl/npm-cache"}}}}
</code></pre>
<p>Approval command from the temp workspace returned:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">✓ Enabled and approved MCP server: everything
</code></pre>
<p>Cursor wrote:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">[
  "everything-154da186314e45d5"
]
</code></pre>
<p><code>cursor-agent mcp list-tools everything</code> succeeded and printed 14 tools:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">Tools for everything (14):
- echo (message)
- get-annotated-message (messageType, includeImage)
- get-env ()
- get-resource-links (count)
- get-resource-reference (resourceType, resourceId)
- get-structured-content (location)
- get-sum (a, b)
- get-tiny-image ()
- gzip-file-as-resource (name, data, outputType)
- simulate-research-query (topic, ambiguous)
- toggle-simulated-logging ()
- toggle-subscriber-updates ()
- trigger-elicitation-request ()
- trigger-long-running-operation (duration, steps)
</code></pre>
<h2>Failed Variants</h2>
<p>Earlier variants are useful negative controls:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Variant</th>
<th>Result</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>user-level <code>~/.cursor/mcp.json</code> only</td>
<td><code>trace: not loaded (needs approval)</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>project config plus <code>--workspace</code>, but command run outside workspace</td>
<td><code>mcp enable trace</code> did not find the server</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>project config from current workspace before approval</td>
<td><code>mcp list-tools trace</code> failed with <code>MCP server "trace" has not been approved</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>project config after approval with 20s timeout</td>
<td>server started, no protocol frame received, timeout killed the process</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>project config after approval with 65s timeout</td>
<td>server started twice, no protocol frame received, Cursor returned MCP timeout</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>official <code>@modelcontextprotocol/server-everything</code> after approval</td>
<td><code>mcp list-tools everything</code> succeeded and listed 14 tools</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2>Conclusions</h2>
<p>This trace upgrades Cursor MCP evidence from static bundle/config discovery to real approval-file behavior:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>mcpServers</code> is the operative project config root for <code>.cursor/mcp.json</code>.</li>
<li><code>mcp enable</code> creates project-scoped approval records in the Cursor project-state directory under HOME.</li>
<li><code>mcp list-tools</code> enforces approval before loading a project MCP.</li>
<li>The standalone <code>mcp list-tools</code> path can complete a no-account stdio MCP handshake when pointed at a known-good server package.</li>
<li>The minimal hand-written stdio fixture still timed out without receiving <code>initialize</code>, so it should not be used as evidence of Cursor protocol failure.</li>
</ul>
<p>The remaining gap is not basic <code>tools/list</code>; it is deeper runtime behavior inside an actual agent/model session: tool invocation policy, permission prompts, auth/OAuth servers, resource access, and how MCP tools appear in model-facing context.</p>

<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/30_grok_mcp_doctor_trace.md</code></h3>
<h1>Grok MCP Doctor Trace</h1>

args = ["-y", "@modelcontextprotocol/server-everything"]
env = { npm_config_cache = "/tmp/grok-mcp-doctor3.jsPmH7/npm-cache" }
enabled = true
</code></pre>

    }

}
</code></pre>

<h2>CLI Add Negative Control</h2>
<p>Two attempts to configure this server through <code>grok mcp add</code> failed because <code>--args -y ...</code> was parsed as an unexpected CLI option:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">error: unexpected argument '-y' found
tip: to pass '-y' as a value, use '-- -y'
</code></pre>
<p>Earlier simple traces confirmed <code>grok mcp add dummy --command /bin/echo --args dummy</code> writes to temp <code>~/.grok/config.toml</code>; this negative control is specific to leading-dash argument passing for <code>npx -y</code>.</p>
<h2>Conclusions</h2>
<ul>
<li>Grok's native TOML <code>mcp_servers.&#x3C;name></code> config can launch a real stdio MCP server in a no-account temp HOME.</li>
<li><code>grok mcp doctor --json</code> performs protocol-level startup validation, not just static config parsing.</li>
<li>The doctor path confirms protocol <code>2025-06-18</code> and tool discovery for a known-good MCP server.</li>
<li>Remote source discovery includes <code>grok.com</code>, but it is skipped without login in this trace.</li>
<li>Remaining MCP gaps are model-session tool invocation, OAuth/HTTP flows, project precedence layering, and plugin-provided MCP activation.</li>
</ul>

<h2>000/00_grand_synthesis.md (발췌)</h2>
<h1>GRAND SYNTHESIS — 5개 코딩 에이전트 × 13개 차원 최종 종합 분석</h1>
<p>이 문서는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code를 13개 아키텍처 차원에서 동시에 비교한 캡스톤 문서다.
개별 비교 문서의 결론을 단순 재배열하지 않고, 서로 다른 설계 철학이 어떤 제품 전략으로 수렴하는지까지 읽어내는 것을 목표로 한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A[5개 에이전트 개요] --> B[13개 차원 비교]
    B --> C[공통 패턴 추출]
    B --> D[핵심 차별점 추출]
    C --> E[기술 선택 시사점]
    D --> E
    E --> F[미래 전망과 설계 교훈]
</code></pre>
<h2>1. 개요</h2>
<h3>이 문서의 목적</h3>
<p>이 문서의 목적은 5개 에이전트를 한 번에 조망할 수 있는 상위 레퍼런스를 만드는 것이다.
개별 문서는 특정 축의 우열을 설명하지만, 실제 제품 선택은 언제나 여러 축의 동시 판단을 요구한다.
따라서 여기서는 TUI, prompt, tool, skill, subagent, app-server, sandbox, config, MCP, memory, plugin, guardian, 그리고 잔여 교차 관심사를 하나의 프레임으로 다시 묶는다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 범위</h3>
<p>범위는 5개 에이전트와 13개 차원이다.
에이전트는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code다.
차원은 TUI, Prompt/Context, Tool Runtime, Skill, Subagents, App-Server Surface, Sandbox, Config, MCP, Memory, Plugin, Guardian, 잔여 교차 관심사(Git/VCS, 모델 라우팅, 에러 처리, 텔레메트리, IDE 통합, 패키징, 테스트, 인증, 멀티모달, 이벤트 시스템, 피처 플래그, 국제화)다.
App-Server 축은 비교 문서 자체가 Codex·Gemini CLI·OpenCode 중심으로 작성되어 있으므로 Aider와 Claude Code는 “의도적 부재”까지 함께 해석한다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[006_app-server-client-surfaces/00_surface]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[008_config-system/00_config]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[010_memory-pipeline/00_memory]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]], [[013_etc/00_etc]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 방법론</h3>
<p>첫째, 각 에이전트 개요 문서에서 기술 스택, 패키지 구조, 핵심 철학을 추출했다.
둘째, 13개 비교 문서에서 축별 우위와 결손, 스카우팅 점수, 디자인 패턴을 수집했다.
셋째, 같은 에이전트가 여러 축에서 반복적으로 보이는 패턴을 묶어 장기 전략으로 재해석했다.
넷째, 단일 승자를 찾기보다 “어떤 상황에서 어떤 설계가 더 설득력 있는가”를 기준으로 실무 추천안을 도출했다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>이 문서를 읽는 방법</h3>
<p>제품 선택이 목적이면 3장, 7장, 8장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
포크나 재구현이 목적이면 2장, 5장, 6장, 9장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
보안 검토가 목적이면 3장, 4장, 8장, 9장을 함께 읽는 편이 낫다.
마지막 부록은 문서 인덱스 역할을 하므로 세부 원문으로 돌아갈 때 사용하면 된다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>
<hr>

<h3>Codex</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: 가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</li>
<li>실무에서 강한 상황: 보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</li>
<li>재구현 관점 한 줄 평: requirements 제약 채널과 prompt fragment provenance를 분리한 구조.</li>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>Aider</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 도구 플랫폼보다 코드 편집 루프에 집중한다. 모델을 좋은 editor로 만드는 쪽에 최적화한다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Python + prompt_toolkit + rich + tree-sitter + Git</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: RepoMap, edit 전략 다양성, git auto-com</li>
</ul>
